[2;36m                    [0m         [39m== libFuzzer crashing input ==[0m                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m===Evaluation [0m[33mReport[0m[39m===[0m                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m# Evaluation Report[0m                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Summary[0m                                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mDuring fuzz testing of the ThreeDXMLParser component with a Jazzer-based harness, a[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mmedium-severity Server-Side Request Forgery [0m[1;39m([0m[39mSSRF[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m issue was detected. The runtime [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39msanitizer intercepted an outbound connection attempt to “jazzer.com:[0m[1;36m443[0m[39m” [0m           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39moriginating from XML processing code. Untrusted input led the parser to initiate a [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39msocket connection, triggering the SSRF check in the Jazzer SSLSocket [0m               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39minstrumentation.[0m                                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Description[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mThe issue arises when the ThreeDXMLParser, invoked by the ThreeDXMLParserFuzzer [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mharness, processes an XML-based 3DXML archive and encounters entity data that [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mcauses the parser to open an [0m[1;35mHTTP[0m[1;39m([0m[39mS[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m connection. The Jazzer security sanitizer [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mreports a medium-severity SSRF violation at the point where java.net.Socket.connect[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mis called. Key observations include:[0m                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m• The stack trace shows XML parsing routines in the JDK’s Xerces implementation [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;39m([0m[39mXMLDocumentFragmentScannerImpl, XMLEntityManager[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m invoked by [0m                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mThreeDXMLParser.parseRoot and related methods.  [0m                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m• The [0m[1;35mHTTP[0m[1;39m([0m[39mS[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m connection sequence begins with Socket.connect and continues through [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mHttpsURLConnectionImpl.getInputStream, indicating that external resource resolution[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mwas triggered during XML entity expansion or similar processing.  [0m                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m• The fuzzer harness [0m[1;39m([0m[39mThreeDXMLParserFuzzer.fuzzerTestOneInput[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m feeds arbitrary [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39minput into the parser, demonstrating that untrusted or maliciously crafted XML can [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mcause outbound network requests.  [0m                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m• The SSRF check failures are reported by [0m                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mcom.code_intelligence.jazzer.sanitizers.ServerSideRequestForgery at two internal [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mcheckpoints [0m[1;39m([0m[39mcheckSsrf, checkSsrfSocket[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m.[0m                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mTo fully understand the scope, an investigation should review:  [0m                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m– ThreeDXMLParser.parseRoot, processZip, and parseContent, focusing on how XML [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mentities or external references are handled.  [0m                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m– The SAXParser or Xerces configuration in use, particularly entity resolution [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39msettings and any custom handlers.  [0m                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m– Code paths that transform parsed XML into resource requests, including any URL [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mopening or stream initialization logic.  [0m                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mThis evaluation highlights that the parser’s handling of external entity or [0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mresource references can be exploited to force network connections based on [0m         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39muntrusted input, amounting to an SSRF vulnerability.[0m                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Initial Issue Log[0m                                                                [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m125[0m[39m:        ZipArchiveEntry rootEntry = [0m[1;35mzipFile.getEntry[0m[1;39m([0m[39mroot[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m126[0m[39m:        if [0m[1;39m([0m[39mrootEntry == null[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m127[0m[39m:            return;[0m                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m128[0m[39m:        [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m129[0m[39m:        SAXParserFactory factory = [0m[1;35mSAXParserFactory.newInstance[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m130[0m[39m:        [0m[1;35mfactory.setNamespaceAware[0m[1;39m([0m[39mtrue[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m131[0m[39m:        [0m                                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m132[0m[39m:        SAXParser parser = null;[0m                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m133[0m[39m:        try [0m[1;39m{[0m                                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m134[0m[39m:            parser = [0m[1;35mfactory.newSAXParser[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m135[0m[39m:        [0m[1;39m}[0m[39m catch [0m[1;39m([0m[39mParserConfigurationException e[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m136[0m[39m:            throw new [0m[1;35mSAXException[0m[1;39m([0m[39me[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m137[0m[39m:        [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m138[0m[39m:[0m                                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m139[0m[39m:        RootHandler rootHandler = new [0m[1;35mRootHandler[0m[1;39m([0m[39mhandler, metadata[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m140[0m[39m:        try [0m[1;39m([0m[39mInputStream is = [0m[1;35mzipFile.getInputStream[0m[1;39m([0m[39mrootEntry[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m141[0m[39m:            [0m[1;35mparser.parse[0m[1;39m([0m[39mis, rootHandler[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m142[0m[39m:        [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m143[0m[39m:    [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mcode[0m[39m>[0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mcode_snippets[0m[39m>[0m                                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Fix Strategy[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<fix_strategy>[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. Root Cause Analysis  [0m                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - The SSRF finding stems from using the JDK’s default SAXParser [0m[1;39m([0m[39mvia  [0m           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;35mSAXParserFactory.newInstance[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m without disabling external entities or setting a [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39msafe entity resolver. As a result, malicious XML can trigger network fetches when [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mresolving external entities.  [0m                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Tika’s core already provides a secure XML parsing utility [0m[1;39m([0m[39mXMLReaderUtils[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mthat configures both the Xerces SecurityManager and an [0m                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mIGNORING_SAX_ENTITY_RESOLVER, preventing DTD loading and external-entity [0m           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mresolution.[0m                                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. Patch Overview  [0m                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   Replace the manual SAXParserFactory instantiation and [0m[1;35mparser.parse[0m[1;39m([0m[33m...[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m call in [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;35mThreeDXMLParser.parseRoot[0m[1;39m([0m[33m...[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m with Tika’s secure parseSAX [0m[1;39m([0m[39mor XMLReader[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m approach.[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mThis change:  [0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Reuses XMLReaderUtils’s secure defaults [0m[1;39m([0m[39mdisallow-doctype, disable external [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mentities, ignore DTDs[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m  [0m                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Preserves the existing RootHandler logic and the ParseContext propagation  [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Eliminates the SSRF vector without touching the fuzzer harness, tests, or [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mutility code outside this module.[0m                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. Detailed Steps  [0m                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   a. In ThreeDXMLParser.java, add the import:  [0m                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      ```java[0m                                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      import org.apache.tika.utils.XMLReaderUtils;[0m                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      ```  [0m                                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   b. Modify [0m[1;35mparseRoot[0m[1;39m([0m[33m...[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m as follows [0m[1;39m([0m[39mpseudo-diff[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m:  [0m                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      ```diff[0m                                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      —   [0m[35m/[0m[35m/[0m[39m current insecure block[0m                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      —   SAXParserFactory factory = [0m[1;35mSAXParserFactory.newInstance[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      —   [0m[1;35mfactory.setNamespaceAware[0m[1;39m([0m[39mtrue[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      —   SAXParser parser = [0m[1;35mfactory.newSAXParser[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      —   RootHandler rootHandler = new [0m[1;35mRootHandler[0m[1;39m([0m[39mhandler, metadata[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      —   try [0m[1;39m([0m[39mInputStream is = [0m[1;35mzipFile.getInputStream[0m[1;39m([0m[39mrootEntry[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      —       [0m[1;35mparser.parse[0m[1;39m([0m[39mis, rootHandler[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      —   [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      +    [0m[35m/[0m[35m/[0m[39m secure parsing using Tika’s XMLReaderUtils[0m                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      +    RootHandler rootHandler = new [0m[1;35mRootHandler[0m[1;39m([0m[39mhandler, metadata[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      +    try [0m[1;39m([0m[39mInputStream is = [0m[1;35mzipFile.getInputStream[0m[1;39m([0m[39mrootEntry[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      +        [0m[35m/[0m[35m/[0m[39m choose one of the secure APIs below:[0m                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      +[0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      +        [0m[35m/[0m[35m/[0m[39m Option [0m[1;36m1[0m[39m: high-level parseSAX [0m[1;39m([0m[39mif available[0m[1;39m)[0m                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      +        [0m[1;35mXMLReaderUtils.parseSAX[0m[1;39m([0m[39mis, rootHandler, metadata, context[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      +[0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      +        [0m[35m/[0m[35m/[0m[39m Option [0m[1;36m2[0m[39m: manual XMLReader parse[0m                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      +        [0m[35m/[0m[35m/[0m[39m XMLReader reader = [0m[1;35mXMLReaderUtils.getXMLReader[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      +        [0m[35m/[0m[35m/[0m[39m [0m[1;35mreader.setContentHandler[0m[1;39m([0m[39mrootHandler[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      +        [0m[35m/[0m[35m/[0m[39m [0m[1;35mreader.parse[0m[1;39m([0m[39mnew [0m[1;35mInputSource[0m[1;39m([0m[39mis[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      +[0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      +    [0m[1;39m}[0m[39m catch [0m[1;39m([0m[39mTikaException e[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      +        throw new [0m[1;35mSAXException[0m[1;39m([0m[32m"Secure XML parsing failed"[0m[39m, e[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      +    [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      ```  [0m                                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   c. Remove the now-unused imports for `javax.xml.parsers.SAXParserFactory` and [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`javax.xml.parsers.SAXParser`, if no longer referenced.  [0m                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   d. Ensure `ParseContext context` is passed into `parseRoot` [0m[1;39m([0m[39mit already is[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m, so [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mthat `parseSAX` has the same context.[0m                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m4[0m[39m. Preserving Functionality  [0m                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - The RootHandler and metadata propagation remain identical; only the parser [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mbackend changes.  [0m                                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Namespaces stay enabled [0m[1;39m([0m[39mXMLReaderUtils respects namespace-aware settings by [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mdefault[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m.  [0m                                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Any higher-level logic in processZip or parseContent is unaffected.[0m            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m5[0m[39m. Side-Effect Considerations  [0m                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - This change tightens XML parsing security by disallowing external [0m             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mDTDs/entities. If any downstream feature legitimately relied on external entity [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mresolution, it would break; however, the rest of Tika also enforces these secure [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mdefaults.  [0m                                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - No other code paths or tests should be affected because external-entity [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39msupport is generally discouraged in Tika and is already disabled in other parsers [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mvia XMLReaderUtils.[0m                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m6[0m[39m. Roll-out & Validation  [0m                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Compile and run existing unit/integration tests to ensure no regressions.  [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Re-run the ThreeDXMLParserFuzzer to confirm that SSRF is no longer triggered [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39munder Jazzer.  [0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Optionally scan the module for any other raw SAXParserFactory uses and apply [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mthe same pattern.[0m                                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mThis strategy mitigates the SSRF risk by leveraging Tika’s proven secure XML [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mparsing utilities, ensuring consistency with the rest of the codebase and [0m          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mpreserving existing behavior for valid documents.  [0m                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mfix_strategy[0m[1m>[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         ===Evaluation [33mEnd[0m===                                                                [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [1;35mcom.example.ThreeDXMLParserFuzzer.parseOne[0m[1;39m([0m[39mThreeDXMLParserFuzzer.jav[0m[1;92ma:65[0m[1;39m)[0m           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        [0m[39mat [0m                                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;35mcom.example.ThreeDXMLParserFuzzer.fuzzerTestOneInput[0m[1;39m([0m[39mThreeDXMLParserFuzzer.jav[0m[1;92ma:39[0m[1;39m)[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mDEDUP_TOKEN: f8a914f52bb68598[0m                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m== libFuzzer crashing input ==[0m                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m===Evaluation [0m[33mReport[0m[39m===[0m                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m# Evaluation Report[0m                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Summary[0m                                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mAn SSRF [0m[1;39m([0m[39mServer-Side Request Forgery[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m issue was discovered when fuzzing [0m            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mThreeDXMLParser via Jazzer. The default SAX parsing path allowed external-entity [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mresolution, triggering an outbound HTTPS connection attempt and tripping Jazzer’s [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mSSRF sanitizer. In an attempt to close this hole, the SAXParser-based code was [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mremoved and replaced with a call to `[0m[1;35mXMLReaderUtils.parseSAX[0m[1;39m([0m[39mis, rootHandler, [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mmetadata, context[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m`. Applying that patch produced a compilation error: there is no [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`parseSAX` overload accepting `[0m[1;39m([0m[39mInputStream, ContentHandler, Metadata, [0m             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mParseContext[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m`. As a result, the build fails in the tika-parser-cad-module.[0m         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Description[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. Initial Issue  [0m                                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - The fuzzer input caused the XML parser in `ThreeDXMLParser.parseContent` [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;39m([0m[39minvoked by the harness[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m to fetch external entities over HTTPS.  [0m                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Jazzer reported a `FuzzerSecurityIssueMedium: Server Side Request Forgery [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;39m([0m[39mSSRF[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` during an attempted connection to `jazzer.com:[0m[1;36m443[0m[39m`.  [0m                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - The stack trace shows the hit originates in the Xerces-based SAX parse path, [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mwithin `XMLDocumentFragmentScannerImpl.scanDocument`, ultimately triggered by [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`[0m[1;35mparser.parse[0m[1;39m([0m[39mis, rootHandler[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m`.[0m                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. Important Observations  [0m                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - The production code in `ThreeDXMLParser` uses a plain [0m                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`[0m[1;35mSAXParserFactory.newInstance[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` and a freshly constructed `SAXParser`.  [0m           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - No custom configuration is applied to disable external entities or DTD [0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mloading.  [0m                                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - The untrusted data [0m[1;39m([0m[39mthe fuzzer input[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m leads to network fetches during XML [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mparsing, flagged as SSRF.[0m                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. Patch Attempt  [0m                                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - The patch removes the manual `SAXParserFactory` and `SAXParser` creation.  [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - The call `[0m[1;35mparser.parse[0m[1;39m([0m[39mis, rootHandler[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` is replaced with:[0m                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     ```java[0m                                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     [0m[1;35morg.apache.tika.utils.XMLReaderUtils.parseSAX[0m[1;39m([0m                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m         is, [0m                                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m         rootHandler, [0m                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m         metadata, [0m                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m         context[0m                                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     [0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     ```[0m                                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - A `TikaException` catch block was added to wrap parsing failures in a [0m         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`SAXException`.[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m4[0m[39m. Patch Result and Build Log  [0m                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Compilation fails with:[0m                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     ```[0m                                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     no suitable method found for [0m[1;35mparseSAX[0m[1;39m([0m                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m       java.io.InputStream,[0m                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m       org.apache.tika.parser.threedxml.ThreeDXMLParser.RootHandler,[0m                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m       org.apache.tika.metadata.Metadata,[0m                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m       org.apache.tika.parser.ParseContext[0m                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     [0m[1;39m)[0m                                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     ```[0m                                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - The two available signatures in `XMLReaderUtils` are:[0m                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     - `[0m[1;35mparseSAX[0m[1;39m([0m[39mInputStream, ContentHandler, ParseContext[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m`[0m                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     - `[0m[1;35mparseSAX[0m[1;39m([0m[39mReader, ContentHandler, ParseContext[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m`[0m                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - There is no four-argument overload accepting a `Metadata`.[0m                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m5[0m[39m. Areas for Further Investigation  [0m                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Review `XMLReaderUtils` to confirm the intended parsing methods and their [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mparameter lists.  [0m                                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Examine how other Tika parsers invoke secure SAX parsing [0m[1;39m([0m[39mespecially those [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mthat disable external entities[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m to see how they pass `Metadata` and `ParseContext`.[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Inspect the definition of `ThreeDXMLParser.RootHandler` to ensure it [0m          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mimplements or wraps `org.xml.sax.ContentHandler`.  [0m                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Check usage of `ParseContext` elsewhere in the CAD module to see how it is [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mconstructed and passed around.  [0m                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Audit any helper utilities in `tika-parsers-standard-modules` for examples of [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39msecure XML parsing without SSRF.[0m                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Initial Issue Log[0m                                                                [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m139[0m[39m:        RootHandler rootHandler = new [0m[1;35mRootHandler[0m[1;39m([0m[39mhandler, metadata[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m140[0m[39m:        try [0m[1;39m([0m[39mInputStream is = [0m[1;35mzipFile.getInputStream[0m[1;39m([0m[39mrootEntry[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m              [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mcode[0m[39m>[0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mcode_snippets[0m[39m>[0m                                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Fix Strategy[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<fix_strategy>[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. Remove manual SAXParser instantiation and usage in the parseRoot method:[0m         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Delete the block creating `SAXParserFactory factory = [0m                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;35mSAXParserFactory.newInstance[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` and the subsequent [0m                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`[0m[1;35mfactory.setNamespaceAware[0m[1;39m([0m[39mtrue[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` and `[0m[1;35mfactory.newSAXParser[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` calls.[0m               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Delete the `SAXParser parser` variable and its associated `[0m[1;35mparser.parse[0m[1;39m([0m[39mis, [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mrootHandler[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` invocation.[0m                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. Replace the old parsing call with Tika’s secure parseSAX API:[0m                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - In `parseRoot`, after instantiating `RootHandler rootHandler = new [0m            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;35mRootHandler[0m[1;39m([0m[39mhandler, metadata[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;`, invoke:[0m                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m       [0m[1;35mXMLReaderUtils.parseSAX[0m[1;39m([0m[39mis, rootHandler, context[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - This three-argument overload will retrieve or create a pooled, secure [0m         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mSAXParser [0m[1;39m([0m[39mwith external-entity resolution disabled[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m and wrap the handler [0m          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mappropriately, preventing SSRF.[0m                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. Adjust exception handling to accommodate the three-argument `parseSAX` [0m          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39msignature:[0m                                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - The three-argument `parseSAX` can throw `TikaException`, `IOException`, and [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`SAXException`. Ensure `parseRoot` catches these:[0m                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m       a. Catch `TikaException` and `IOException` and rethrow as `SAXException`, [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mpreserving the message and root cause.[0m                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m       b. Propagate any `SAXException` unchanged.[0m                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - This aligns with existing `parseContent`[0m[35m/[0m[39m`parse` method signatures and reuses [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mthe wrapping pattern already employed for other parsing steps [0m[1;39m([0m[39me.g., manifest [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mparsing[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m.[0m                                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m4[0m[39m. Ensure `RootHandler` remains unchanged, as it already implements/extends [0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`ContentHandler` and writes to `Metadata`. The `Metadata` passed to its constructor[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mwill continue to be populated internally, eliminating the need to pass it directly [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mto `parseSAX`.[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m5[0m[39m. Verify consistency with `processZip`:[0m                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Since `processZip` already calls `[0m[1;35mXMLReaderUtils.parseSAX[0m[1;39m([0m[39mis, manifestHandler,[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mcontext[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m`, mimic its exception handling and invocation style in `parseRoot`.[0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mRationale:[0m                                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Switching to the three-argument `XMLReaderUtils.parseSAX` removes SSRF exposure [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mby disabling external-entity resolution and leveraging Tika’s pooled secure [0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mparsers.[0m                                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- By matching the existing pattern in `processZip`, this approach compiles cleanly [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;39m([0m[39mthe correct overload exists[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m and preserves existing functionality [0m[1;39m([0m[39mmetadata [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mextraction via the handler[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m.[0m                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Exception handling is aligned with other parts of the module, ensuring that [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mparsing errors remain consistent and that no broad exception swallowing occurs.[0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- No harness, test, or external library code is modified; only the CAD parser’s [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39minternal parsing logic changes.[0m                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Potential side effects: [0m[3;35mNone[0m[39m expected beyond the desired hardening; the metadata [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mextraction logic in `RootHandler` is untouched and will continue to operate on the [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mSAX event stream as before.[0m                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mCode Range to Patch:[0m                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<code_range>tika-parsers/tika-parsers-standard/tika-parsers-standard-modules/tika-p[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39marser-cad-module/src/main/java/org/apache/tika/parser/threedxml/ThreeDXMLParser.jav[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;92ma:125[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m145[0m[39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mcode_range[0m[39m>[0m                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mfix_strategy[0m[1m>[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         ===Evaluation [33mEnd[0m===                                                                [2m                [0m
